Low: 30{\/p} Tuesday: {\/strong}Wintry mix to snow in the morning. Dry for the afternoon. Mostly cloudy and breezy.  High: 36 {\/p} Rain will return through the afternoon from the south. A wintry mix to snow is likely to fall late this afternoon across the far northwest. Rain, heavy at times, continues through this evening as temperatures slowly fall through the 30s. Rain will mix with snow and even freezing rain overnight, before changing all over to snow Tuesday morning. Freezing rain is most likely along I-71 and areas north of there. Highest snow totals will be found across the far northwest. Less than an inch is possible for the rest of the Tri-State. Rain totals will range from around a quarter of an inch to the far northwest, to over an inch across the far southeast. By Tuesday morning, roads will be worse in the far northwest. There may be some slick or lightly snow covered roads around Cincinnati. Roads should fair better across the far south and southeast. Morning snow showers and flurries are likely Tuesday before ending. The afternoon remains dry, but will be chilly, with wind chills in the 20s.
